\bentry
\word[jack(1)]{jack}
\pron{jAYxkf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
jAYxku: 
\banum
\alnum{a} etutxga; BAra etutxva yaMtarx. 
\alnum{b} Ure etutxga; vAhanada cakarxvanunx cokakxTa mADalu yA badalAyisalu acacxnunx meVletitx hiDiyuva salakaraNe, etutxva sAdhana.  \imglink{jackfigure}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage width 0.8cm height 0.6cm {J_Pictures/jack.jpg}}} 
\alnum{c} gaDiyAradalilx gaMTeyanunx bArisuva, mAnavAkArada boMbe. 
\alnum{d} meVTukaDiDx; hApfRsikADfR modalAda vAdayxgaLalilx taMtiyanunx miDiyalu aLavaDisiruva salakaraNe. 
\alnum{e}  = \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{cheapjack(1)}{$^1$cheapjack}. 
\alnum{f}  = \hyperref{kandict_l.pdf}{L}{lumberjack}{lumberjack}. 
\alnum{g}  = \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{steeplejack}{steeplejack}. 
\alnum{h} halavu yaMtarx modalAdavugaLa BAgagaLa hesaru. 
\alnum{i}  = \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{bootjack}{bootjack}. 
\alnum{j} (muMtAda cikakx athavA puTaTx) peYkf miVnu. 
\alnum{k} (boVlfsx ATa) (ATagAraru guriyiDabeVkAda) puTaTx biLi ceMDu. 
\alnum{l} (\bava dalilx, \Eva vAgi parxyoVga) kalilxna athavA loVhada saNaNx goVligaLiMda ADuva oMdu ATa. 
\alnum{m} (kelavu jAti pArxNigaLalilx) gaMDupArxNi. 
\alnum{n} (\ashi) patetxVdAra; poliVsinavanu. 
\alnum{o} (\ame) (\ashi) haNa. 
\alnum{p} gulAma; manuSayxna, muKayxvAgi seYnikana, poVSAku toTiTxruva seVvaka, \mo vara citarxviruva isipxVTele. 
\alnum{q} viduyxnamxMDalavanunx saMpakiRsuva sAdhana. 
\alnum{r} \eng{(Jack) (John} eMbudara badalu baLasuva \rUpa) shirxVsAmAnayx athavA yAvudeV jAtiya pArxNiya gaMDu. 
\eanum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{everyman jack} parxtiyobabxnU; parxtiyobabx gaMDasU. 
\numi{2} \eng{Jack and Jill} 
\banum
\alnum{a} poVrapoVri; huDuga huDugi. 
\alnum{b} gaMDu heNuNx; gaMDasu heMgasu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} \eng{jack of all trades} sakala kAyaRpaTu; savaRkAyaR nipuNa; elalx kelasagaLanUnx mADabalalxvanu; yAvudeV kasubu mADabalalxvanu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{before you could say Jack Robinson} `jAyxkf rAbinfsanf' enunxvaSaTxralilxyeV, enunxvaSaTxkUkx muMceyeV; bahaLa beVgane athavA kUDaleV. 
\num{2} \eng{on one's jack (\engit{also}, on one's Jack Jones)} (\ashi) oMTiyAgi; obobxMTiganAgi. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\num{1} (poVkarf ATa) BAri bAji; [eraDu gulAma (jAki) athavA inUnx utatxmavAda elegaLuLaLx ATagAranu] bAcikoLuLxva bAji haNada (paMtha paNada) motatx. 
\hyperdef{J}{jackpot(2)}{} 
\num{2} (yAvudeV adaqSaTx pariVkeSxyalilx athavA lATariyalilx gedudxkoMDa) BAri bahumAna. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\eng{hit the jackpot} 
\banum
\alnum{a} BAri bahumAnavanunx hoDeduko, gedudxko. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) tiVra adaqSaTxshAliyAgiru. 
\eanum
\emng

\bentry
\word[jam(1)]{jam}
\pron{jAYxmf}
\gl{\kirx}
\expl{(\vakaq\ \eng{jamming}, \BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{jammed}).}
\bmng
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (eraDu talagaLa madheyx vasutxvanunx) amuku; jaDi; turuku; iruku; aDaku. 
\num{2} (yaMtarx BAgavanunx) kelasakekx bAradaMte -- irukisu, adumi biDu, jajijx biDu. 
\num{3} yaMtarxvanunx adumi biTuTx kelasa mADadaMte mADu. 
\num{4} (vasutxgaLu otAtxgi mudedxyAguvaMte) adumu; giDi. 
\num{5} (vasutxvanunx, ikakxTuTx jAga \mo vugaLa oLakekx) balavAgi -- taLuLx, turuku, nUku, giDi, jaDi. 
\num{6} (mAgaR \mo vanunx) kikikxridu tuMbi, neredu, seVri -- aDacibiDu, baMdf mADi biDu. \eng{7} (reVDiyoV) adumu; iruku; saMmadiRsu (samAna taraMgAMtaradalilx reVDiyoV alegaLanunx parxsAra mADi anayxra reVDiyoV athavA reVDArf saMkeVtagaLanunx) gajibiji mADu. 
\num{8} nigaRmanavanunx -- taDe, niroVdhisu: \eng{we were jammed in} horabaradaMte namamxnunx taDeyalAyitu. 
\num{9} (\sA\ \eng{jam on}) (berxVkugaLu \mo vugaLanunx) balavaMtavAgi athavA idadxkikxdadxMte -- amuku, hAku, otutx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (beNe hAkidaMte) bigiyAgi sikikxko, irukiko, aDaciko. 
\num{2} (yaMtarxda \vi) yaMtarxda BAgavu aDaci(koMDiruvudariMda) kelasa mADadaMte Agiru. 
\num{3} (jAyxsf \saM). (\AmA) (hosa layagatigaLanunx seVrisikoLuLxtAtx) samaya sUPxtiRyiMda hADu; tatAkxlada utAsxhadiMda hADu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[jam(2)]{jam}
\pron{jAYxmf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} otatxDa; iruku; aDacu. 
\num{2} (otatxDa \mo vugaLiMda yaMtarx \mo vu) aDacikoLuLxvudu; aDacihoVgi niMtubiDuvudu. 
\num{3} (jana, vAhana, \mo vugaLa) nUku nugagxlu; kikikxrida neravi; saMmadaR: \eng{traffic jam} vAhana saMmadaR. 
\num{4} (\AmA) ikakxTuTx; piVkalATa; PajiVti; uBayasaMkaTa: \eng{owing to a thoughtless act I am in a jam} oMdu avicArada kelasadiMdAgi nAniVga piVkalATadalilx sikikxkoMDidedxVne. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[jam(3)]{jam}
\pron{jAYxmf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} jAYxmu; murababx; sakakxrepAkadalilx kudisi rasAyanadaMte mADida haNuNx. 
\num{2} (\birx) (\AmA) savidinisu; ahitavAdudanunx maresuva, hitakaravU sulaBavU Ada vasutx (\rUpa\ saha): \eng{this job is not all jam} I kelasa saMpUNaRvAgi hitakaravAdudeVnalalx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\eng{real jam} sAvxrasayx; savi; suKavanUnx mAdhuyaRvanUnx koDuvaMthadudx: \eng{without real jam, cash and kisses, the world is a bitter pill} kAMcana matutx cuMbanadaMtha sAvxrasayxgaLilalxdidadxre, I loVkavoMdu kahi guLige. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[job(1)]{job}
\pron{jAbf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\kanmu\ kUligAgiyoV parxtiPalakAkxgiyoV mADuva) cUrugelasa; puDigelasa; cilalxre kelasa. 
\num{2} (\ashi) aparAdha; tapipxta; \kanmu\ koLeLx, daroVDe, sulige. 
\num{3} (\kanmu\ utatxmavAgi mADida) kelasa; duDimeya pariNAma; sharxmada Pala. 
\num{4} sAvxthaRsAdhane; sAvxthaR sAdhaka -- kAyaR, udayxma; savxMta lABakAkxgi kataRvayxvanunx, sAvaRjanika hitavanunx, baligoDuva vayxvahAra. 
\num{5} (saMbaLada) udoyxVga; hudedx; cAkari; nwkari. 
\num{6} (\AmA) kataRvayx; mADaleVbeVkAda kAyaR, kelasa. 
\num{7} (\AmA) sharxmada, parxyAsada -- kelasa. 
\num{8} (kaMpUyxTarf) parxteyxVkavAgi parigaNisida oMdu kAyaR. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{bad job} 
\banum
\alnum{a} viPala kAyaR; (duDidadedxlalx) vayxthaRvAda kelasa: (duDimeyelalx) maNuNxpAlAda kelasa; (parisharxmavelalx) vayxthaRvAda kAyaR. 
\alnum{b} ataqpitxkaravAda sithxti; duHsithxti: hadageTaTx parisithxti. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{good job} susithxti; oLeLxya parisithxti; taqpitxkara parisithxti. 
\num{3} \eng{jobs for the boys} (\AmA) tananx beMbaligarige (parxtiPalavAgi) koDabahudAda lABakaravAda, anukUlakaravAda kelasagaLu, hudedxgaLu. 
\num{4} \eng{just the job} (\ashi) (vasutx, kelasa, \mo vugaLa \vi) yAvudu beVkoV adeV; bayasidedxV. 
\num{5} \eng{make a good job of} (keYgoMDa) kelasavanunx cenAnxgi, taqpitxkaravAgi, samapaRkavAgi -- mADu. 
\num{6} \eng{make the best of a bad job} ataqpitxkara parisithxtiyalUlx keYlAdadadxnunx, sAdhayxvAdudanunx mADu. 
\numi{7} \eng{on the job} 
\banum
\alnum{a} kelasadalilx toDagi; kelasamADutAtx; kAyaRniratanAgi. 
\alnum{b} leYMgikakirxyeyalilx toDagi; saMBoVgisutAtx. 
\eanum
\numie

\bentry
\word[job(2)]{job}
\pron{jAbf}
\gl{\kirx}
\bmng
(\vakaq\ \eng{jobbing}, \BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{jobbed}).
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} (\birx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (kudure, baMDi, \mo vanunx gotAtxda kelasakekx athavA avadhige) bADigege tegeduko. 
\alnum{b} I riVti bADigege koDu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (baMDavALa patarxgaLa athavA sATxkfgaLa) daLALxLi vAyxpAra mADu; daLALxLi -- vayxvahAra naDesu (\akirx\ saha). 
\num{3} (baMDavALa patarxgaLu matutx sarakugaLu, \mo vanunx) koLuLx matutx mAru (\akirx\ saha). 
\num{4} naMbi vahisida adhikArasAthxnavanunx sAvxthaRkAkxgi durupayoVga paDisiko. 
\num{5} (oMdu \vi\ athavA vayxvahAradalilx) aniVtiyiMda vatiRsu; duvayxRvahAra mADu; duvAyxRpAra mADu. 
\num{6} (\ashi) moVsamADu; ToVpihAku; vaMcisu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} saNaNxpuTaTx kelasa, cilalxregelasa, puDigelasa athavA biDigelasa -- mADu. 
\num{2} (naMbi vahisida kelasavanunx) sAvxthaRkAkxgi baLasiko, durupayoVga mADiko. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng

\bentry
\word[joke(1)]{joke}
\pron{joVkf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum

\noindent

\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{make a \eng{joke} about} (oMdara, obabxna viSayavAgi) hAsayxmADu; geVli mADu; tamASe mADu; laGuvAgi athavA hAsayxvAgi mAtanADu. 
\hyperdef{J}{joke(1) pagu(2)}{} 
\num{2} \eng{no \eng{joke}} huDugATada viSayavalalx, tamASeyalalx; gurutaravAda viSaya: \eng{it is no \eng{joke}} adeVnU tamASeyalalx; adu gaMBiVravAda viSaya, kelasa. 
\num{3} \eng{play a joke on (one)} (obabxnanunx) hAsayxkekx, tamASege guri mADu; hAsAyxsapxdavAgisu. 
\hyperdef{J}{joke(1) pagu(4)}{} 
\num{4} \eng{practical \eng{joke}} kucoVdayx; kuceVSeTx; obabxnanunx nagepATalu mADaleMdeV avana meVle mADida kuceVSeTx. 
\num{5} \eng{standing joke} hAsAyxsapxda; saripaDisalu sAdhayxveV ilalxdaSuTx hAsAyxsapxdavAda viSaya, saMgati, parisithxti, vayxkitx, \mo vu. 
\num{6} \eng{the \eng{joke} of the town} UrigeV hAsAyxsapxdavAda, nagegeVDiyAda -- vayxkitx, viSaya. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[jump(1)]{jump}
\pron{jaMpf }
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (neladiMda) negeta; eguru; hArike; cimumxvike; kupapxLike; kupapxLa; laMGana. 
\num{2} becicx biVLuvudu; hwhAruvudu; cakitagoLuLxvudu; saMBarxma, duguDa athavA AGAtadiMda Aguva becucx. 
\num{3} (mobalagu, bele, dara, mwlayx, \mo vugaLa) thaTaTxneya Erike; haThAtf hecacxLa; Akasimxka teVji. 
\num{4} EkAEkiya badalAvaNe; haThAtf parivataRne. 
\num{5} laMGana; hArike; negeta; atikarxmaNa; saraNi, vAda, \mo vugaLalilx anukarxmavAgi muMduvareyade, idadxkikxdadxMte naDuvaNa haMtagaLanunx, GaTaTxgaLanunx atikarxmisi hArida aMtara. 
\num{6} (kudure \mo vu) hArabeVkAgiruva -- aDiDx, aDacaNe. 
\num{7}  = \hyperlink{jump bid}{jump bid}.

\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\eng{the jumps} (\ashi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (ati kuDitadiMdAguva) kaMpana saninx(pAta); ede naDuka; haqdayakaMpana. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) ede naDuka; ede DavaguTuTxvudu; haqdayakaMpana; parxbalaBiVti: \eng{this place fairly gives me the jumps} I jAga nanage ede naDuka huTiTxsutatxde, barisutatxde. 
\eanum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{get the jump on (\engit{also}, have the jump on)} (\ashi) (edurALiya hUTavanunx muninxriVkiSxsi avananunx) miVrisuva -- avakAsha paDe, dorakisiko.

\bentry

\bentry
\word[just(2)]{just}
\pron{jasfTx}
\gl{\kirxvi}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} sariyAgi; niSakxqqSaTxvAgi; karAruvAkAkxgi: \eng{just at that spot } sariyAgi A sathxLadalelxV; adeV sathxLadalelxV. \eng{just then} A hotitxge sariyAgi. \eng{just three O'clock} Iga sariyAgi mUru gaMTe; Iga tAneV, idiVga, inUnx -- mUru gaMTe aSeTxV. \eng{just as I opened the door} nAnu bAgilu tegeyuvudakekx sariyAgi; nAnu bAgilu tegeyutitxdadxMte. \eng{just what I want} nAnu bayasidedxV; nAneVnu bayasutetxVneyoV adeV. 
\num{2} hAgeyeV; aMteyeV; sariyAgi: \eng{just as you say} niVnu heVLidaMteyeV. 
\num{3} adeV; adeVneV; adeVyeV: \eng{that is just it} hwdu adeV; vivAdadalilxruva aMsha adeVne. 
\num{4} (niKaravAda samAcAravanunx keVLuva parxshAnxthaRka padagaLa joteyalilx) \eng{just how did you do it?} adanunx heVgetAneV mADide? \eng{I wonder just how good he is} avanu eSaTxramaTiTxge oLeLxyavaneMdu athavA samathaRneMdu nAnu kwtukapaDutetxVne. 
\num{5} keVvala aSuTx mAtarx; tAvanAmxtarx; eSuTx beVkoV, avashayxkavoV aSeTxV: \eng{I just managed it} aSuTx mAtarxdalelxV, aSaTXralelxV heVgoV adanunx niBAyiside. \eng{I just saw him} (\birx) avananunx keVvala noVDide aSeTxV. \eng{(wait) just a minute, please} dayaviTuTx oMdeV oMdu nimiSa, oMdu nimiSamAtarx taDeyiri. 
\num{6} idiVga; Iga tAneV; Iga savxlapx hotitxnalilx; A samayakekx sariyAgi athavA savxlapx hecucx kaDime A hotitxge: \eng{I have just seen him} (\birx) avananunx Iga tAneV noVDide. 
\num{7} (\AmA) keVvala; iSeTxV; aSeTxV: \eng{it's just that I don't like him } nanage avana viSayadalilx olavilalx, aSeTx; nanage avananunx kaMDare Aguvudilalx, aSeTx. \eng{we are just good friends} nAvu oLeLxya senxVhitaru aSeTx. \eng{it just doesn't make sense} adaralelxVnU, adakekxVnU -- athaRvilalx, aSeTx. \eng{just listen to that cheering}! A jayakAravanunx savxlapx keVLu, Alisu! 
\num{8} oMdiSuTx; savxlapx: \eng{just (you) wait till I catch you} nAnu ninanxnunx hiDiyuvavaregU, nanage niVnu sikukxvavaregU -- oMdiSuTx taDe, savxlapx tALu. 
\num{9} (\AmA) nijakUkx; KaMDita(vAgiyU); nijavAgiyU: \eng{it is just splendid} adu nijakUkx aduBxtavAgide. 
\num{10} saMpUNaRvAgi; pUtiRyAgi; savaRthA: \eng{not just yet} inUnx (pUtiR) ilalx; IgaleV inUnx ilalx athavA alalx; inUnx Agilalx. \eng{it is just as well that I checked} IgaleV nAnu (adanunx) pariVkiSxsidare oLeLxyadu. 
\num{11} (\ashi) (avadhAraNAthaRdalilx) sariyAgi; nijavAgi; satayxvAgi; KacitavAgi; nishicxtavAgi: \eng{won't I just give him a pasting}! nAnavanige sariyAgi koDitxVnoV ilalxvoV noVDutitxru.

\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum

\banum
